(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced that Emmanuel Babeau, age 53, has been appointed to succeed Martin G. King as Chief Financial Officer, effective May 1, 2020.  Mr. King will assume the role of CEO, PMI America, effective May 1, 2020. The change of Mr. King&#8217;s role is not a result of any disagreement with the Company on any matter.  The compensation of Mr. King in his new role will be determined at a later date.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Mr.&#160;Babeau has served at Schneider Electric SE, a French multinational corporation </span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;color:#222222;">specializing in energy and automation digital solutions,</span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"> in various executive capacities since 2009, most recently, as Deputy CEO in charge of Finance and Legal Affairs. </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Pursuant to his employment agreement, Mr.&#160;Babeau&#8217;s compensation will be as follows: </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;-sec-extract:summary;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br/></span></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</span></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Mr. Babeau will be granted a sign-on equity grant with a fair market value of CHF 3,300,000 (or $ 3,423,750)</span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">1</sup></span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"> consisting of 40% restricted share units (RSUs) and 60% performance share units (PSUs); and</span></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</span></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Mr. Babeau will be granted a sign-on RSU award with a fair market value of CHF 5,000,000 (or $ 5,187,500).</span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">1</sup>&#160;</span></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#160;</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Mr. Babeau will be entitled to severance if his employment is terminated without Cause (as defined in the agreement).  Depending on the timing of such termination, Mr. Babeau would be entitled to a lump sum cash payment of up to two times his base salary and his incentive compensation award (which could be prorated). His RSUs will vest fully and his PSUs will vest on a prorated basis as scheduled and certified by the Compensation and Leadership Development Committee of the Board of Directors. Any severance under this agreement is conditioned on a 24-month non-compete obligation and is subject to the Company&#8217;s clawback policy.</span></div><div It corresponds to the current Company practice, that the Company keeps the right to change at any time without notice or compensation.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Fidelity Premium</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;">For each completed year of service, the Company pays a cumulative bonus of CHF 150.-- on each anniversary of the Effective Date, up to a maximum of CHF 3,000.-- for 20 years of service.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Termination of Employment</font><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial Narrow;font-size:11pt;">This contract shall be terminable in accordance with Swiss law. 4500</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#262626;">E. corey.henry@pmi.com</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:132%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:center;font-size:14pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:14pt;color:#262626;font-weight:bold;">Emmanuel Babeau Joins Philip Morris International as CFO</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">LAUSANNE,&#160;Switzerland&#8212;March 2, 2020&#8212;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#262626;">Philip Morris International Inc. (PMI) (NYSE: PM) </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">announced today that Emmanuel Babeau has been appointed Chief Financial Officer, replacing Martin King. King will be taking on a new role as CEO, PMI America, a newly created function. Reporting to global CEO Andr&#233; Calantzopoulos, King</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#262626;">&#32;will coordinate both international services based in the U.S. and all U.S. representation, including PMI&#8217;s relationship with Altria, which is commercializing </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#262626;font-style:italic;">IQOS</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#262626;">&#32;in the American market.</font></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">Emmanuel Babeau will join PMI on May 1, 2020 from Schneider Electric, where he served most recently as Deputy CEO in charge of Finance and Legal Affairs. A native of France and graduate of ESCP Business School, he has spent nearly three decades leading fundamental change across industries.</font></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">&#8220;PMI is undergoing a period of intensive change as we transition away from cigarettes to our science-based smoke-free products&#8212;products that are much better alternatives than continued cigarette smoking,&#8221; said Andr&#233; Calantzopoulos. &#8220;We are thrilled that Emmanuel will be joining us to further accelerate the PMI transformation towards a smoke-free future. He has an enviable track record of challenging the status quo and growing businesses under the most complex circumstances.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">During his 10 years at Schneider Electric, Babeau helped to grow the company from &#8364;18 billion market cap to c. &#8364;60 billion, while transforming the business model from hardware products for electrical distribution into digital technologies driving the energy transition and industry 4.0. In 2019, Harvard Business Review cited Schneider Electric as one of the top 15 business transformations of the past decade. The company now has &#8364;27 billion in revenues and is a leader in digital solutions for efficiency and sustainability.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">Earlier, Babeau spent 15 years at Pernod Ricard, including six years as Group CFO, where he helped to turn a regional challenger into the world&#8217;s second-largest wine and spirits company. That transformation involved several important acquisitions, including Seagram and Allied Domecq, which brought to Pernod Ricard iconic wine and spirit brands such as Chivas Regal, Martell, Malibu, and Mumm.</font></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">Emmanuel Babeau commented: &#8220;PMI is precisely the challenge I was looking for: a global leader in its industry with a commitment to fundamental change&#8212;and one that is prompted not only by business strategy but also by a desire to operate more sustainably and in the interest of public health. I am </font></div><div><br></div><div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><a name="se4d2a91931234e679b87d53c963a5ebe"></a></div><div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">excited about working with Andr&#233; Calantzopoulos, Jacek Olczak, and the rest of the leadership team to achieve PMI&#8217;s business objectives.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;">Babeau sits on the boards of Sodexo, Sanofi, and AVEVA PLC. In his new position, he will report to Andr&#233; Calantzopoulos.</font></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:132%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;font-size:10.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;font-weight:bold;">Philip Morris International: Delivering a Smoke-Free Future</font></div><div style="line-height:132%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;font-size:10.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">Philip Morris International (PMI) is leading a transformation in the tobacco industry to create a smoke-free future and ultimately replace cigarettes with smoke-free products to the benefit of adults who would otherwise continue to smoke, society, the company, and its shareholders. PMI is a leading international tobacco company engaged in the manufacture and sale of cigarettes, as well as smoke-free products and associated electronic devices and accessories, and other nicotine-containing products in markets outside the United States. In addition, PMI ships a version of its&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;font-style:italic;">IQOS&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">Platform 1 device and its consumables authorized by the U.S. Food and Drug Administration to Altria Group, Inc. for sale in the United States under license. PMI is building a future on a new category of smoke-free products that, while not risk-free, are a much better choice than continuing to smoke. Through multidisciplinary capabilities in product development, state-of-the-art facilities, and scientific substantiation, PMI aims to ensure that its smoke-free products meet adult consumer preferences and rigorous regulatory requirements. PMI's smoke-free&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;font-style:italic;">IQOS</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">&#160;product portfolio includes heat-not-burn and nicotine-containing vapor products. As of December&#160;31, 2019, PMI estimates that approximately 9.7 million adult smokers around the world have already stopped smoking and switched to PMI's heat-not-burn product</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;font-style:italic;">,</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">&#160;available for sale in 52 markets in key cities or nationwide under the&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;font-style:italic;">IQOS&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">brand. For more information, please visit&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;text-decoration:underline;">www.pmi.com</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">&#160;and&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;text-decoration:underline;">www.pmiscience.com</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10.5pt;color:#262626;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:130%;padding-bottom:8px;padding-top:8px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;background-color:#ffffff;color:#222222;"># # #</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div></div>	</div></body>
